vāyavīyasaṃhitā
atha śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamī vāyavīyasaṃhitā prārabhyate 
śrīgaṇeśāya namaḥ 
śrīgaurīśaṃkarābhyāṃ namaḥ 
atha saptamī vāyavīyasaṃhitā prārabhyate 
Chapter 
vyāsa uvāca
namaśśivāya somāya sagaṇāya sasūnave  ŚivPab
pradhānapuruṣeśāya sargasthityaṃtahetave  ŚivPcd
śaktirapratimā yasya hyaiśvaryaṃ cāpi sarvagam  ŚivPab
svāmitvaṃ ca vibhutvaṃ ca svabhāvaṃ saṃpracakṣate  ŚivPcd
tamajaṃ viśvakarmāṇaṃ śāśvataṃ śivamavyayam  ŚivPab
mahādevaṃ mahātmānaṃ vrajāmi śaraṇaṃ śivam  ŚivPcd
dharmakṣetre mahātīrthe gaṃgākāliṃdisaṃgame  ŚivPab
prayāge naimiṣāraṇye brahmalokasya vartmani  ŚivPcd
munayaśśaṃsitātmānaḥ satyavrataparāyaṇāḥ  ŚivPab
mahaujaso mahābhāgā mahāsatraṃ vitenire  ŚivPcd
tatra satraṃ samākarṇya teṣāmakliṣṭakarmaṇām  ŚivPab
sākṣātsatyavatīsūnorvedavyāsasya dhīmataḥ  ŚivPcd
śiṣyo mahātmā medhāvī triṣu lokeṣu viśrutaḥ  ŚivPab
pañcāvayavayuktasya vākyasya guṇadoṣavit  ŚivPcd
uttarottaravaktā ca bruvato 'pi bṛhaspateḥ  ŚivPab
madhuraḥ śravaṇānāṃ ca manojñapadaparvaṇām  ŚivPcd
kathānāṃ nipuṇo vaktā kālavinnayavitkaviḥ  ŚivPab
ājagāma sa taṃ deśaṃ sūtaḥ paurāṇikottamaḥ  ŚivPcd
taṃ dṛṣṭvā sūtamāyāṃtaṃ munayo hṛṣṭamānasāḥ  ŚivPab
tasmai sāma ca pūjāṃ ca yathāvatpratyapādayan  ŚivPcd
pratigṛhya satāṃ pūjāṃ munibhiḥ pratipāditām  ŚivPab
uddiṣṭamānasaṃ bheje niyukto yuktamātmanaḥ  ŚivPcd
tatastatsaṃgamādeva munīnāṃ bhāvitātmanām  ŚivPab
sotkaṃṭhamabhavaccitaṃ śrotuṃ paurāṇikīṃ kathām  ŚivPcd
tadā tamanukūlābhirvāgbhiḥ pūjya  maharṣayaḥ  ŚivPab
atīvābhimukhaṃ kṛtvā vacanaṃ cedamabruvan  ŚivPcd
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
romaharṣaṇa sarvajña bhavānno bhāgyagauravāt  ŚivPab
saṃprāptodya mahābhāga śaivarāja mahāmate  ŚivPcd
purāṇavidyāmakhilāṃ vyāsātpratyakṣamīyivān  ŚivPab
tasmādāścaryabhūtānāṃ kathānāṃ tvaṃ hi bhājanam  ŚivPcd
ratnānāmurusārāṇāṃ ratnākara ivārṇavaḥ  ŚivPab
yacca bhūtaṃ yacca bhavyaṃ yaccānyadvastu vartate  ŚivPcd
na tavāviditaṃ kiñcittriṣu lokeṣu vidyate  ŚivPab
tvamadṛṣṭavaśādasmaddarśanārthamihāgataḥ  ŚivPcd
akurvankimapi śreyo na vṛthā gantumarhasi  ŚivPef
tasmācchrāvyataraṃ puṇyaṃ satkathājñānasaṃhitam  ŚivPab
vedāṃtasārasarvasvaṃ purāṇaṃ śrāvayāśu naḥ  ŚivPcd
evamabhyarthitassūto munibhirvedavādibhiḥ  ŚivPab
ślakṣṇāṃ ca nyāyasaṃyuktāṃ pratyuvāca śubhāṃ giram  ŚivPcd a
sūta uvāca
pūjito 'nugṛhītaśca bhavadbhiriti coditaḥ  ŚivPab
kasmātsamyaṅna vibrūyāṃ purāṇamṛṣipūjitam  ŚivPcd
abhivaṃdya mahādevaṃ devīṃ skaṃdaṃ vināyakam  ŚivPab
naṃdinaṃ ca tathā vyāsaṃ sākṣātsatyavatīsutam  ŚivPcd
vakṣyāmi paramaṃ puṇyaṃ purāṇaṃ vedasaṃmitam  ŚivPab
śivajñānārṇavaṃ sākṣādbhaktimuktiphalapradam  ŚivPcd
śabdārthanyāyasaṃyuktai rāgamārthairvibhūṣitam  ŚivPab
śvetakalpaprasaṃgena vāyunā kathitaṃ purā  ŚivPcd
vidyāsthānāni sarvāṇi purāṇānukramaṃ tathā  ŚivPab
tatpurāṇasya cotpattiṃ bruvato me nibodhata  ŚivPcd
aṃgāni vedāścatvāro mīmāṃsānyāyavistaraḥ  ŚivPab
purāṇaṃ dharmaśāstraṃ ca vidyāścetāścaturdaśa  ŚivPcd
āyurvedo dhanurvedo gāṃdharvaścetyanukramāt  ŚivPab
arthaśāstraṃ paraṃ tasmādvidyā hyaṣṭādaśa smṛtāḥ  ŚivPcd
aṣṭādaśānāṃ vidyānāmetāsāṃ bhinnavartmanām  ŚivPab
ādikartā kavissākṣācchūlapāṇiriti śrutiḥ  ŚivPcd
sa hi sarvajagannāthaḥ sisṛkṣurakhilaṃ jagat  ŚivPab
brahmāṇaṃ vidadhe sākṣātputramagre sanātanam  ŚivPcd
tasmai prathamaputrāya brahmaṇe viśvayonaye  ŚivPab
vidyāścemā dadau pūrvaṃ viśvasṛṣṭyarthamīśvaraḥ  ŚivPcd
pālanāya hariṃ devaṃ rakṣāśaktiṃ dadau tataḥ  ŚivPab
madhyamaṃ tanayaṃ viṣṇuṃ pātāraṃ brahmaṇo 'pi hi  ŚivPcd
labdhavidyena vidhinā prajāsṛṣṭiṃ vitanvatā  ŚivPab
prathamaṃ sarvaśāstrāṇāṃ purāṇaṃ brahmaṇā smṛtam  ŚivPcd
anaṃtaraṃ tu vaktrebhyo vedāstasya vinirgatāḥ  ŚivPab
pravṛttissarvaśāstrāṇāṃ tanmukhādabhavattataḥ  ŚivPcd
yadāsya vistaraṃ śaktā nādhigaṃtuṃ prajā bhuvi  ŚivPab
tadā vidyāsamāsārthaṃ viśveśvaraniyogataḥ  ŚivPcd
dvāparāṃteṣu viśvātmā viṣṇurviśvaṃbharaḥ prabhuḥ  ŚivPab
vyāsanāmnā caratyasminnavatīrya mahītale  ŚivPcd
evaṃ vyastāśca vedāśca dvāparedvāpare dvijāḥ  ŚivPab
nirmitāni purāṇāni anyāni ca tataḥ param  ŚivPcd
sa punardvāpare cāsminkṛṣṇadvaipāyanākhyayā  ŚivPab
araṇyāmiva havyāśī satyavatyāmajāyata  ŚivPcd
saṃkṣipya sa punarvedāṃścaturdhā kṛtavānmuniḥ  ŚivPab
vyastavedatayā loke vedavyāsa iti śrutaḥ  ŚivPcd
purāṇānāñca saṃkṣiptaṃ caturlakṣapramāṇataḥ  ŚivPab
adyāpi devaloke tacchatakoṭipravistaram  ŚivPcd
yo vidyāccaturo vedān sāṃgopaṇiṣadāndvijaḥ  ŚivPab
na cetpurāṇaṃ saṃvidyānnaiva sa syādvicakṣaṇaḥ  ŚivPcd
itihāsapurāṇābhyāṃ vedaṃ samupabṛṃhayet  ŚivPab
bibhetyalpaśrutādvedo māmayaṃ pratariṣyati  ŚivPcd
sargaśca pratisargaśca vaṃśo manvaṃtarāṇi ca  ŚivPab
vaṃśānucaritaṃ caiva purāṇaṃ pañcalakṣaṇam  ŚivPcd
daśadhā cāṣṭadhā caitatpurāṇamupadiśyate  ŚivPab b
bṛhatsūkṣmaprabhedena munibhistattvavittamaiḥ  ŚivPcd
brāhmaṃ pādmaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ ca śaivaṃ bhāgavataṃ tathā  ŚivPab
bhaviṣyaṃ nāradīyaṃ ca mārkaṃḍeyamataḥ param  ŚivPcd
āgneyaṃ brahmavaivartaṃ laiṃgaṃ vārāhameva ca  ŚivPab
skāndaṃ ca vāmanaṃ caiva kaurmyaṃ mātsyaṃ ca gāruḍam  ŚivPcd
brahmāṃḍaṃ ceti puṇyo 'yaṃ purāṇānāmanukramaḥ  ŚivPab
tatra śaivaṃ turīyaṃ yacchārvaṃ sarvārthasādhakam  ŚivPcd
graṃtho lakṣapramāṇaṃ tadvyastaṃ dvādaśasaṃhitam  ŚivPab
nirmitaṃ tacchivenaiva tatra dharmaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ  ŚivPcd
taduktenaiva dharmeṇa śaivāstraivarṇikā narāḥ  ŚivPab
tasmādvimukutimanvicchañcchivameva samāśrayet  ŚivPcd
tamāśrityaiva devānāmapi muktirna cānyathā  ŚivPab
yadidaṃ śaivamākhyātaṃ purāṇaṃ vedasaṃmitam  ŚivPab
tasya bhedānsamāsena bruvato me nibodhata  ŚivPcd
vidyeśvaraṃ tathā raudraṃ vaināyakamanuttamam  ŚivPab
aumaṃ mātṛpurāṇaṃ ca rudraikādaśakaṃ tathā  ŚivPcd
kailāsaṃ śatarudraṃ ca śatarudrākhyameva ca  ŚivPab
sahasrakoṭirudrākhyaṃ vāyavīyaṃ tataḥparam  ŚivPcd
dharmasaṃjñaṃ purāṇaṃ cetyevaṃ dvādaśa saṃhitāḥ  ŚivPab
vidyeśaṃ daśasāhasramuditaṃ graṃthasaṃkhyayā  ŚivPcd
raudraṃ vaināyakaṃ caumaṃ mātṛkākhyaṃ tataḥ param  ŚivPab
pratyekamaṣṭasāhasraṃ trayodaśasahasrakam  ŚivPcd
raudrakādaśakākhyaṃ yatkailāsaṃ ṣaṭsahasrakam  ŚivPab
śatarudraṃ trisāhasraṃ koṭirudraṃ tataḥ param  ŚivPcd
sahasrairnavabhiryuktaṃ sarvārthajñānasaṃyutam  ŚivPab
sahasrakoṭirudrākhyamekādaśasahasrakam  ŚivPcd
catussahasrasaṃkhyeyaṃ vāyavīyamanuttamam  ŚivPab
dharmasaṃjñaṃ purāṇaṃ yattaddvādaśasahasrakam  ŚivPcd
tadevaṃ lakṣamuddiṣṭaṃ śaivaṃ śākhāvibhedataḥ  ŚivPab
purāṇaṃ vedasāraṃ tadbhuktimuktiphalapradam  ŚivPcd
vyāsena tattu saṃkṣiptaṃ caturviṃśatsahasrakam  ŚivPab
śaivantatra purāṇaṃ vai caturthaṃ saptasaṃhitam  ŚivPcd
vidyeśvarākhyā tatrādyā dvitīyā rudrasaṃhitā  ŚivPab
tṛtīyā śatarudrākhyā koṭirudrā caturthikā  ŚivPcd
pañcamī kathitā comā ṣaṣṭhī kailāsasaṃhitā  ŚivPab
saptamī vāyavīyākhyā saptaivaṃ saṃhitā iha  ŚivPcd
vidyeśvaraṃ dvisāhasraṃ raudraṃ pañcaśatāyutam  ŚivPab
triṃśattathā dvisāhasraṃ sārdhaikaśatamīritam  ŚivPcd
śatarudrantathā koṭirudraṃ vyomayugādhikam  ŚivPab
dvisāhasraṃ ca dviśataṃ tathomaṃ bhūsahasrakam  ŚivPcd
catvāriṃśatsāṣṭaśataṃ kailāsaṃ bhūsahasrakam  ŚivPab
catvāriṃśacca dviśataṃ vāyavīyamataḥ param  ŚivPcd
catussāhasrasaṃkhyākamevaṃ saṃkhyāvibhedataḥ  ŚivPab
śrutamparamapuṇyantu purāṇaṃ śivasaṃjñakam  ŚivPcd
catuḥsāhasrakaṃ yattu vāyavīyamudīritam  ŚivPab
tadidaṃ vartayiṣyāmi bhāgadvayasamanvitam  ŚivPcd
nāvedaviduṣe vācyamidaṃ śāstramanuttamam  ŚivPab
na caivāśraddhadhānāya nāpurāṇavide tathā  ŚivPcd
parīkṣitāya śiṣyāya dhārmikāyānasūyave  ŚivPab
pradeyaṃ śivabhaktāya śivadharmānusāriṇe  ŚivPcd
purāṇasaṃhitā yasya prasādānmayi vartate  ŚivPab
namo bhagavate tasmai vyāsāyāmitatejase  ŚivPcd
iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ pūrvakhaṇḍe vidyāvatārakathanaṃ nāmaprathamo 'dhyāyaḥ

sūta uvāca
purā kālena mahatā kalpetīte punaḥpunaḥ  ŚivPab
asminnupasthite kalpe pravṛtte sṛṣṭhikarmaṇi  ŚivPcd
pratiṣṭhitāyāṃ vārtāyāṃ prabuddhāsu prajāsu ca  ŚivPab
munīnāṃ ṣaṭkulīyānāṃ bruvatāmitaretaram  ŚivPcd
idaṃ paramidaṃ neti vivādassumahānabhūt  ŚivPab
parasya durnirūpatvānna jātastatra niścayaḥ  ŚivPcd
te 'bhijagmurvidhātāraṃ draṣṭuṃ brahmāṇamavyayam  ŚivPab
yatrāste bhagavān brahmā stūyamānassurāsuraiḥ  ŚivPcd
meruśṛṃge śubhe ramye devadānavasaṃkule  ŚivPab
siddhacāraṇasaṃvāde yakṣagaṃdharvasevite  ŚivPcd
vihaṃgasaṃghasaṃghuṣṭe maṇividrumabhūṣite  ŚivPab
nikuṃjakaṃdaradarīgṛhānirjharaśobhite  ŚivPcd
tatra brahmavanaṃ nāma nānāmṛgasamākulam  ŚivPab
daśayojanavistīrṇaṃ śatayojanamāyatam  ŚivPcd
surasāmalapānīyapūrṇaramyasarovaram  ŚivPab
mattabhramarasaṃchannaramyapuṣpitapādapam  ŚivPcd
taruṇādityasaṃkāśaṃ tatra cāru mahatpuram  ŚivPab
durdharṣabaladṛptānāṃ daityadānavarakṣasām  ŚivPcd
taptajāṃbūnadamayaṃ prāṃśuprākāratoraṇam  ŚivPab
nirvyūhavalabhīkūṭapratolīśatamaṃḍitam  ŚivPcd
mahārhamaṇicitrābhirlelihānamivāṃbaram  ŚivPab
mahābhavanakoṭībhiranekābhiralaṃkṛtam  ŚivPcd
tasminnivasati brahmā sabhyaiḥ sārdhaṃ prajāpatiḥ  ŚivPab
tatra gatvā mahātmānaṃ sākṣāllokapitāmaham  ŚivPcd
daddaśurmunayo devā devarṣigaṇasevitam  ŚivPab
śuddhacāmīkaraprakhyaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam  ŚivPcd
prasannavadanaṃ saumyaṃ padmapatrāyatekṣaṇam  ŚivPab
divyakāṃtisamāyuktaṃ divyagaṃdhānulepanam  ŚivPcd
divyaśuklāṃbaradharaṃ divyamālāvibhūṣitam  ŚivPab
surāsurendrayogīṃdravaṃdyamānapadāṃbujam  ŚivPcd
sarvalakṣaṇayuktāṃgyā labdhacāmarahastayā  ŚivPab
bhrājamānaṃ sarasvatyā prabhayeva divākaram  ŚivPcd
taṃ dṛṣṭvā munayassarve prasannavadanekṣaṇāḥ  ŚivPab
śirasyaṃjalimādhāya tuṣṭuvussurapuṃgavam  ŚivPcd
munaya ūcuḥ
namastrimūrtaye tubhyaṃ sargasthityaṃtahetave  ŚivPab
puruṣāya purāṇāya brahmaṇe paramātmane  ŚivPcd
namaḥ pradhānadehāya pradhānakṣobhakāriṇe  ŚivPab
trayoviṃśatibhedena vikṛtāyāvikāriṇe  ŚivPcd
namo brahmāṇḍadehāya brahmāṃḍodaravartine  ŚivPab
tatra saṃsiddhakāryāya saṃsiddhakaraṇāya ca  ŚivPcd
namostu sarvalokāya sarvalokavidhāyine  ŚivPab
sarvātmadehasaṃyoga viyogavidhihetave  ŚivPcd
tvayaiva nikhilaṃ sṛṣṭaṃ saṃhṛtaṃ pālitaṃ jagat  ŚivPab
tathāpi māyayā nātha na vidmastvāṃ pitāmaha  ŚivPcd
sūta uvāca
evaṃ brahmā mahābhāgairmaharṣibhirabhiṣṭutaḥ  ŚivPab
prāha gaṃbhīrayā vācā munīn prahlādayanniva  ŚivPcd
brahmovāca
ṛṣayo he mahābhāgā mahāsattvā mahaujasaḥ  ŚivPab
kimarthaṃ sahitāssarve yūyamatra samāgatāḥ  ŚivPcd
tamevaṃvādinaṃ devaṃ brahmāṇaṃ brahmavittamāḥ  ŚivPab
vāgbhirvinayagarbhābhissarve prāṃjalayo 'bruvan  ŚivPcd
munaya ūcuḥ
bhagavannaṃdhakāreṇa mahatā vayamāvṛtāḥ  ŚivPab
khinnā vivadamānāśca na paśyāmo 'tra yatparam  ŚivPcd
tvaṃ hi sarvajagaddhātā sarvakāraṇakāraṇam  ŚivPab
tvayā hyaviditaṃ nātha neha kiṃcana vidyate  ŚivPcd
kaḥ pumān sarvasattvebhyaḥ purāṇaḥ puruṣaḥ paraḥ  ŚivPab
viśuddhaḥ paripūrṇaśca śāśvataḥ parameśvaraḥ  ŚivPcd
kenaiva citrakṛtyena prathamaṃ sṛjyate jagat  ŚivPab
tattvaṃ vada mahāprājña svasaṃdehāpanuttaye  ŚivPcd
evaṃ pṛṣṭastadā brahmā vismayasmeravīkṣaṇaḥ  ŚivPab
devānāṃ dānavānāṃ ca munīnāmapi sannidhau  ŚivPcd
utthāya suciraṃ dhyātvā rudra ityuddharan girim  ŚivPab
ānaṃdaklinnasarvāṃgaḥ kṛtāṃjalirabhāṣata  ŚivPcd
iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ pūrvakhaṇḍe muniprastāvavarṇanaṃ nāma dvitīyo 'dhyāyaḥ
Chapter 
brahamovāca
yato vāco nivartaṃte aprāpya manasā saha  ŚivPab
ānaṃdaṃ yasya vai vidvānna bibheti kutaścana  ŚivPcd
yasmātsarvamidaṃ brahmaviṣṇurudrendrapūrvakam  ŚivPab
saha bhūtendriyaiḥ sarvaiḥ prathamaṃ saṃprasūyate  ŚivPcd
kāraṇānāṃ ca yo dhātā dhyātā paramakāraṇam  ŚivPab
na saṃprasūyate 'nyasmātkutaścana kadācana  ŚivPcd
sarvaiśvaryeṇa saṃpanno nāmnā sarveśvaraḥ svayam  ŚivPab
sarvairmumukṣubhirdhyeyaśśaṃbhurākāśamadhyagaḥ  ŚivPcd
yo 'gre māṃ vidadhe putraṃ jñānaṃ ca prahiṇoti me  ŚivPab
tatprasādānmayālabdhaṃ prājāpatyamidaṃ padam  ŚivPcd
īśo vṛkṣa iva stabdho ya eko divi tiṣṭhati  ŚivPab
yenedamakhilaṃ pūrṇaṃ puruṣeṇa mahātmanā  ŚivPcd a
eko bahūnāṃ jaṃtūnāṃ niṣkriyāṇāṃ ca sakriyaḥ  ŚivPab
ya eko bahudhā bījaṃ karoti sa maheśvaraḥ  ŚivPcd
jīvairebhirimāṃllokānsarvānīśo ya īśate   ŚivPab
ya eko bhāgavānrudro na dvitīyo 'sti kaścana  ŚivPcd
sadā janānāṃ hṛdaye saṃniviṣṭo 'pi yaḥ paraiḥ  ŚivPab
alakṣyo lakṣayanviśvamadhitiṣṭhati sarvadā  ŚivPcd
yastu kālātpramuktāni kāraṇānyakhilānyapi  ŚivPab
anantaśaktirevaiko bhagavānadhitiṣṭhati  ŚivPcd
na yasya divaso rātrirna samāno na cādhikaḥ  ŚivPab
svabhāvikī parāśaktirnityā jñānakriye api  ŚivPcd
yadidaṃ kṣaramavyaktaṃ yadapyamṛtamakṣaram  ŚivPab
tāvubhāvakṣarātmānāveko devaḥ svayaṃ haraḥ  ŚivPcd
īśate tadabhidhyānādyojanāsattvabhāvanaḥ  ŚivPab
bhūyo hyasya paśorante viśvamāyā nivartate  ŚivPcd
yasminna bhāsate vidyunna sūryo na ca candramāḥ  ŚivPab
yasya bhāsā vibhātīdamityeṣā śāśvatī śrutiḥ  ŚivPcd
eko devo mahādevo vijñeyastu maheśvaraḥ  ŚivPab
na tasya paramaṃ kiṃcitpadaṃ samadhigamyate  ŚivPcd

nābhijātyaṃ na vai śīlaṃ na balaṃ na ca naipuṇam  ŚivPab
bhavetkāryāya paryāptaṃ kālaśca hyanirodhakaḥ  ŚivPcd
ye sanāthāśca dātāro gītavādyairupasthitāḥ  ŚivPab
ye cānāthāḥ parānnādāḥ kālasteṣu samakriyaḥ  ŚivPcd
phalaṃtyakāle na rasāyanāni samyakprayuktānyapi cauṣadhāni  ŚivPab
tānyeva kālena samāhṛtāni siddhiṃ prayāṃtyāśu sukhaṃ diśaṃti  ŚivPcd a
nākālato 'yaṃ mriyate jāyate vā nākālataḥ puṣṭimagryāmupaiti  ŚivPab
nākālataḥ sukhitaṃ duḥkhitaṃ vā nākālikaṃ vastu samasti kiṃcit  ŚivPcd
kālena śītaḥ prativāti vātaḥkālena vṛṣṭirjaladānupaiti  ŚivPab
kālena coṣmā praśamaṃ prayāti kālena sarvaṃ saphalatvameti  ŚivPcd
kālaśca sarvasya bhavasya hetuḥ kālena sasyāni bhavaṃti nityam  ŚivPab
kālena sasyāni layaṃ prayāṃti kālena saṃjīvati jīvalokaḥ  ŚivPcd
itthaṃ kālātmanastattvaṃ yo vijānāti tattvataḥ  ŚivPab
kālātmānamatikramya kālātītaṃ sa paśyati  ŚivPcd
na yasya kālo na ca baṃdhamuktī na yaḥ pumānna prakṛtirna viśvam  ŚivPab
vicitrarūpāya śivāya tasmai namaḥparasmai parameśvarāya  ŚivPcd
iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ pūrvakhaṇḍe kālamahimavarṇanaṃ nāma saptamo 'dhyāyaḥ
Chapter 
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
kena mānena kālesminnāyussaṃkhyā prakalpyate  ŚivPab
saṃkhyārūpasya kālasya kaḥ punaḥ paramo 'vadhiḥ  ŚivPcd

abde pañca sahasrāṇi catvāriṃśadyutāni ca  ŚivPab

aharaṃte pralīyante rātryante viśvasaṃbhavaḥ  ŚivPcd

Chapter 
munaya ūcuḥ
kathaṃ jagadidaṃ kṛtsnaṃ vidhāya ca nidhāya ca  ŚivPab

somanandīti vikhyātastasmādeṣa samākhyayā  ŚivPcd

bhūṣayāmāsa tandivyairbhūṣaṇai ratnabhūṣitaiḥ  ŚivPcd

vāyuruvāca
nivedayāmi jagato vāgarthātmyaṃ kṛtaṃ yathā  ŚivPab

kalābhistāni tattvāni vyāptānyeva yathātatham  ŚivPcd
parasyāḥ prakṛterādau pañcadhā pariṇāmataḥ  ŚivPab
kalāśca tā nivṛttyādyā vyāptāḥ pañca yathottaram  ŚivPcd

śaktyādi ca pṛthivyantaṃ śivatattvasamudbhavam  ŚivPab
vyāptamekena tenaiva mṛdā kuṃbhādikaṃ yathā  ŚivPcd

vṛthā pariśramastasya nirayāyaiva kevalam  ŚivPcd

śaktirājñā parā śaivī cidrūpā marameśvarī  ŚivPab
śivo 'dhitiṣṭhatyakhilaṃ yayā kāraṇabhūtayā  ŚivPcd

tasmācchivaḥ paro hetustasyājñā parameśvarī  ŚivPcd

devastrīṣu ca deveṣu dakṣasyādhvarakāraṇāt  ŚivPab
vīreṇa vīrabhadreṇa na hi kaścidadaṇḍitaḥ  ŚivPcd

vāyuruvācva
parokṣamaparokṣaṃ ca dvividhaṃ jñānamiṣyate  ŚivPab
parokṣamasthiraṃ prāhuraparokṣaṃ tu susthiram  ŚivPcd
hetūpadeśagamyaṃ yattatparokṣaṃ pracakṣate  ŚivPab b

nāparokṣādṛte mokṣa iti kṛtvā viniścayam  ŚivPab

tatrāpi mūlamaṃtro 'yaṃ kiṃcidbhedasamanvayāt  ŚivPab
tatrāpi pañcamo varṇo dvādaśasvarabhūṣitaḥ  ŚivPcd
tāsmādanena maṃtreṇa manovākkāyabhedataḥ  ŚivPab
āvayorarcanaṃ kuryājjapahomādikaṃ tathā  ŚivPcd

yathāśakti yathāsaṃpadyathāyogaṃ yathārati  ŚivPcd
yadā kadāpi vā bhaktyā yatra kutrāpi vā kṛtā  ŚivPab
yena kenāpi vā devi pūjā muktiṃ nayiṣyate  ŚivPcd
mayyāsaktena manasā yatkṛtaṃ mama sundari  ŚivPab
matpriyaṃ ca śivaṃ caiva krameṇāpyakrameṇa vā  ŚivPcd
tathāpi mama bhaktā ye nātyaṃtavivaśāḥ punaḥ  ŚivPab
teṣāṃ sarveṣu śāstreṣu mayeva niyamaḥ kṛtaḥ  ŚivPcd
tatrādau saṃpravakṣyāmi mantrasaṃgrahaṇaṃ śubham  ŚivPab
yaṃ vinā niṣphalaṃ jāpyaṃ yena vā saphalaṃ bhavet  ŚivPcd
oṃ iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe pañcākṣaramāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma trayodaśo 'dhyāyaḥ

śrīkṛṣṇa uvāca
bhagavānmaṃtramāhātmyaṃ bhavatā kathitaṃ prabho  ŚivPab
tatprayogavidhānaṃ ca sākṣācchrutisamaṃ yathā  ŚivPcd

upamanyuruvāca

saṃskāraṃ paramaṃ puṇyaṃ śivena patibhāṣitam  ŚivPcd
samyak kṛtādhikāraḥ syātpūjādiṣu naro yataḥ  ŚivPab

sā dīkṣā śāṃbhavī proktā sā punarbhidyate dvidhā  ŚivPab

yayā syānnirvṛtiḥ sadyassaiva tīvratarā matā  ŚivPab b
tīvrā tu jīvatotyaṃtaṃ puṃsaḥ pāpaviśodhikā  ŚivPcd

yo 'nyathā kurute mohātsa vinaśyati durmatiḥ  ŚivPab
tasmātsarvaprakāreṇa guruḥ śiṣyaṃ parīkṣayet  ŚivPcd

sā yasmātparamā śaktiḥ prabodhānaṃdarūpiṇī  ŚivPcd
ānaṃdabodhayorliṃgamaṃtaḥkaraṇavikriyāḥ  ŚivPab
yathā syātkaṃparomāṃcasvaranetrāṃgavikriyāḥ  ŚivPcd

tatsaṃparkaiḥ śivārcādau saṃgatairvātha tadgataiḥ  ŚivPcd
śiṣyastu śikṣaṇīyatvādgurorgauravakāraṇāt  ŚivPab
tasmātsarvaprayatnena gurorgauravamācaret  ŚivPcd
yo gurussa śivaḥ prokto yaḥ śivaḥ sa guruḥ smṛtaḥ  ŚivPab
gururvā śiva evātha vidyākāreṇa saṃsthitaḥ  ŚivPcd
yathā śivastathā vidyā yathā vidyā tathā guruḥ  ŚivPab

sarvadevātmakaścāsau sarvamaṃtramayo guruḥ  ŚivPab
tasmātsarvaprayatnena yasyājñāṃ śirasā vahet  ŚivPcd
śreyo 'rthī yadi gurvājñāṃ manasāpi na laṃghayet  ŚivPab
gurvājñāpālako yasmājjñānasaṃpattimaśnute  ŚivPcd
gacchaṃstiṣṭhansvapanbhuṃjannānyatkarma samācaret  ŚivPab
samakṣaṃ yadi kurvīta sarvaṃ cānujñayā guroḥ  ŚivPcd
gurorgṛhe samakṣaṃ vā na yatheṣṭāsano bhavet  ŚivPab
gururdevo yataḥ sākṣāttadgṛhaṃ devamandiram  ŚivPcd
pāpināṃ ca yathā saṃgāttatpāpātpatito bhavet  ŚivPab
yatheha vahnisaṃparkānmalaṃ tyajati kāṃcanam  ŚivPcd
tathaiva gurusaṃparkātpāpaṃ tyajati mānavaḥ  ŚivPab
yathā vahnisamīpastho ghṛtakumbho vilīyate  ŚivPcd
tathā pāpaṃ vilīyeta hyācāryasya samīpataḥ  ŚivPab
yathā prajvalito vahniḥ śuṣkamārdraṃ ca nirdahet  ŚivPcd
tathāyamapi saṃtuṣṭo guruḥ pāpaṃ kṣaṇāddahet  ŚivPab

ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi śivāśramaniṣeviṇām  ŚivPab
śivaśāstroktamārgeṇa naimittikavidhikramam  ŚivPcd
sarveṣvapi ca māseṣu pakṣayorubhayorapi  ŚivPab a
aṣṭābhyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃ tathā parvāṇi ca kramāt  ŚivPcd

jyeṣṭhe mūlākhyanakṣatre śītakumbhaṃ pradāpayet  ŚivPcd

Chapter 
upamanyuruvāca

tattattattvādhipāmeva mūrtiṃ sthūlāṃ viciṃtayet  ŚivPab
sadāśivāṃtā brahmādyabhavādyāścāṣṭamūrtayaḥ  ŚivPcd
śivasya mūrtayaḥ sthūlāḥ śivaśāstre viniścitāḥ  ŚivPab
ghorā miśrā praśāntāśca mūrtayastā munīśvaraiḥ  ŚivPcd
phalābhilāṣarahitaiścintyāścintāviśāradaiḥ  ŚivPab
ghorāścecciṃtitāḥ kuryuḥ pāparogaparikṣayam  ŚivPcd
cireṇa miśre saumye tu na sadyo na cirādapi  ŚivPab
saumye muktirviśeṣeṇa śāṃtiḥ prajñā prasidhyati  ŚivPcd
sidhyaṃti siddhayaścātra kramaśo nātra saṃśayaḥ  ŚivPab
oṃ iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe yogagatau vighnotpattivarṇanaṃ nāmāṣṭatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
Chapter 
upamanyuruvāca
śrīkaṃṭhanāthaṃ smaratāṃ sadyaḥ sarvārthasiddhayaḥ  ŚivPab
prasidhyaṃtīti matvaike taṃ vai dhyāyaṃti yoginaḥ  ŚivPcd
sthityarthaṃ manasaḥ kecitsthūladhyānaṃ prakurvate  ŚivPab
sthūlaṃ tu niścalaṃ ceto bhavetsūkṣme tu tatsthiram  ŚivPcd
śive tu ciṃtite sākṣātsarvāḥ sidhyanti siddhayaḥ  ŚivPab
mūrtyaṃtareṣu dhyāteṣu śivarūpaṃ viciṃtayet  ŚivPcd
lakṣayenmanasaḥ sthairyaṃ tattaddhyāyetpunaḥ punaḥ  ŚivPab
dhyānamādau saviṣayaṃ tato nirviṣayaṃ jaguḥ  ŚivPcd
tatra nirviṣayaṃ dhyānaṃ nāstītyeva satāṃ matam  ŚivPab

tena nirviṣayā buddhiḥ kevaleha pravartate  ŚivPab
tasmātsaviṣayaṃ dhyānaṃ bālārkakiraṇāśrayam  ŚivPcd
sūkṣmāśrayaṃ nirviṣayaṃ nāparaṃ paramārthataḥ  ŚivPab
yadvā saviṣayaṃ dhyānaṃ tatsākārasamāśrayam  ŚivPcd
nirākārātmasaṃvittirdhyānaṃ nirviṣayaṃ matam  ŚivPab
nirbījaṃ ca sabījaṃ ca tadeva dhyānamucyate  ŚivPcd
nirākāraśrayatvena sākārāśrayatastathā  ŚivPab
tasmātsaviṣayaṃ dhyānamādau kṛtvā sabījakam  ŚivPcd
aṃte nirviṣayaṃ kuryānnirbījaṃ sarvasiddhaye  ŚivPab
prāṇāyāmena sidhyaṃti devyāḥ śāṃtyādayaḥ kramāt  ŚivPcd
śāṃtiḥ praśāṃtirdīptiśca prasādaśca tataḥ param  ŚivPab
śamaḥ sarvāpadāṃ caiva śāṃtirityabhidhīyate  ŚivPcd b
tamaso 'ntabahirnāśaḥ praśāntiḥ parigīyate  ŚivPab
bahirantaḥprakāśo yo dīptirityabhidhīyate  ŚivPcd
svasthatā yā tu sā buddhaḥ prasādaḥ parikīrtitaḥ  ŚivPab
kāraṇāni ca sarvāṇi sabāhyābhyaṃtarāṇi ca  ŚivPcd
buddheḥ prasādataḥ kṣipraṃ prasannāni bhavantyuta  ŚivPab
dhyātā dhyānaṃ tathā dhyeyaṃ yadvā dhyānaprayojanam  ŚivPcd
etaccatuṣṭayaṃ jñātvā dhyātā dhyānaṃ samācaret  ŚivPef
jñānavairāgyasaṃpanno nityamavyagramānasaḥ  ŚivPab
śraddadhānaḥ prasannātmā dhyātā sadbhirudāhṛtaḥ  ŚivPcd
dhyai ciṃtāyāṃ smṛto dhātuḥ śivaciṃtā muhurmuhuḥ  ŚivPab
yogābhyāsastathālpe 'pi yathā pāpaṃ vināśayet  ŚivPab
dhyāyataḥ kṣaṇamātraṃ vā śraddhayā parameśvaram  ŚivPcd
avyākṣiptena manasā dhyānamityabhidhīyate  ŚivPab
buddhipravāharūpasya dhyānasyāsyāvalaṃbanam  ŚivPab
dhyeyamityucyate sadbhistacca sāṃbaḥ svayaṃ śivaḥ  ŚivPcd
vimuktipratyayaṃ pūrṇamaiśvaryaṃ cāṇimādikam  ŚivPab
śivadhyānasya pūrṇasya sākṣāduktaṃ prayojanam  ŚivPcd
yasmātsaukhyaṃ ca mokṣaṃ ca dhyānādabhayamāpnuyāt  ŚivPab
tasmātsarvaṃ parityajya dhyānayukto bhavennaraḥ  ŚivPcd
nāsti dhyānaṃ vinā jñānaṃ nāsti dhyānamayoginaḥ  ŚivPab
dhyānaṃ jñānaṃ ca yasyāsti tīrṇastena bhavārṇavaḥ  ŚivPcd

yathāvahnirmahādīptaḥ śuṣkamārdraṃ ca nirdahet  ŚivPab
tathā śubhāśubhaṃ karma dhyānāgnirdahate kṣaṇāt  ŚivPcd
atyalpo 'pi yathā dīpaḥ sumahannāśayettamaḥ  ŚivPab
yogābhyāsastathālpo 'pi mahāpāpaṃ vināśayet  ŚivPcd
dhyāyataḥ kṣaṇamātraṃ vā śraddhayā parameśvaram  ŚivPab
yadbhavetsumahacchreyastasyāṃto naiva vidyate  ŚivPcd
nāsti dhyānasamaṃ tīrthaṃ nāsti dhyānasamaṃ tapaḥ  ŚivPab
nāsti dhyānasamo yajñastasmāddhyānaṃ samācaret  ŚivPcd
tīrthāni toyapūrṇāni devānpāṣāṇamṛnmayān  ŚivPab
yogino na prapadyaṃte svātmapratyayakāraṇāt  ŚivPcd
yogināṃ ca vapuḥ sūkṣmaṃ bhavetpratyakṣamaiśvaram  ŚivPab
yathā sthūlamayuktānāṃ mṛtkāṣṭhādyaiḥ prakalpitam  ŚivPcd
yathehāṃtaścarā rājñaḥ priyāḥ syurna bahiścarāḥ  ŚivPab
tathāṃtardhyānaniratāḥ priyāśśaṃbhorna karmiṇaḥ  ŚivPcd
bahiskarā yathā loke nātīva phalabhoginaḥ  ŚivPab a
dṛṣṭvā narendrabhavane tadvadatrāpi karmiṇaḥ  ŚivPcd
yadyaṃtarā vipadyaṃte jñānayogārthamudyataḥ  ŚivPab
yogasyodyogamātreṇa rudralokaṃ gamiṣyati  ŚivPcd
anubhūya sukhaṃ tatra sa jāto yogināṃ kule  ŚivPab
jñānayogaṃ punarlabdhvā saṃsāramativartate  ŚivPcd
jijñāsurapi yogasya yāṃ gatiṃ labhate naraḥ  ŚivPab
na tāṃ gatimavāpnoti sarvairapi mahāmakhaiḥ  ŚivPcd
dvijānāṃ vedaviduṣāṃ koṭiṃ saṃpūjya yatphalam  ŚivPab
bhikṣāmātrapradānena tatphalaṃ śivayogine  ŚivPcd
yajñāgnihotradānena tīrthahomeṣu yatphalam  ŚivPab
yogināmannadānena tatsamastaṃ phalaṃ labhet  ŚivPcd
ye cāpavādaṃ kurvaṃti vimūḍhāśśivayoginām  ŚivPab
śrotṛbhiste prapadyante narakeṣvāmahīkṣayāt  ŚivPcd
sati śrotari vaktāsyādapavādasya yoginām  ŚivPab
tasmācchrotā ca pāpīyāndaṇḍyassumahatāṃ mataḥ  ŚivPcd
ye punaḥ satataṃ bhaktyā bhajaṃti śavayoginaḥ  ŚivPef
te vidaṃti mahābhogānaṃte yogaṃ ca śāṃkaram  ŚivPab
bhogārthibhirnaraistasmātsaṃpūjyāḥ śivayoginaḥ  ŚivPcd
pratiśrayānnapānādyaiḥ śayyāprāvaraṇādibhiḥ  ŚivPab
yogadharmaḥ sasāratvādabhedyaḥ pāpamudgaraiḥ  ŚivPcd
vajrataṃdulavajjñeyaṃ tathā pāpena yoginaḥ  ŚivPab
na lipyaṃte ca tāpaughaiḥ padmapatraṃ yathāṃbhasā  ŚivPcd
yasmindeśe vasennityaṃ śivayogarato muniḥ  ŚivPab
so 'pi deśo bhavetpūtaḥ sapūta iti kiṃ punaḥ  ŚivPcd
tasmātsarvaṃ parityajya kṛtyamanyadvicakṣaṇaḥ  ŚivPab
sarvaduḥkhaprahāṇāya śivayogaṃ samabhyaset  ŚivPcd
siddhayogaphalo yogī lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā  ŚivPab
bhogānbhuktvā yathākāmaṃ viharedvātra vartatām  ŚivPcd
athavā kṣudramityeva matvā vaiṣayikaṃ sukham  ŚivPab
tyaktvā virāgayogena svecchayā karma mucyatām  ŚivPcd
yastvāsannāṃ mṛtiṃ martyo dṛṣṭāriṣṭaṃ ca bhūyasā  ŚivPab
sa yogārambhanirataḥ śivakṣetraṃ samāśrayet  ŚivPcd
sa tatra nivasanneva yadi dhīramanā naraḥ  ŚivPab
prāṇānvināpi rogādyaiḥ svayameva parityajet  ŚivPcd
kṛtvāpyanaśanaṃ caiva hutvā cāṃgaṃ śivānale  ŚivPab
kṣiptvā vā śivatīrtheṣu svadehamavagāhanāt  ŚivPcd
śivaśāstroktavidhivatprāṇānyastu parityajet  ŚivPab
sadya eva vimucyeta nātra kāryā vicāraṇā   ŚivPcd
rogādyairvātha vivaśaḥ śivakṣetraṃ samāśritaḥ  ŚivPab
mriyate yadi sopyevaṃ mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ  ŚivPcd
 udyogaṃ kurvata ityarthaḥ
 na cāsāvātmaghātaka iti pāṭhāntaram b

śāstraviśraṃbhadhīreṇa manasā kriyate yataḥ  ŚivPcd
śivanindārataṃ hatvā pīḍitaḥ svayameva vā  ŚivPab
yastyajeddustyajānprāṇānna sa bhūyaḥ prajāyate  ŚivPcd
śivanindārataṃ haṃtumaśakto yaḥ svayaṃ mṛtaḥ  ŚivPab
sadya eva pramucyeta triḥ saptakulasaṃyutaḥ  ŚivPcd
śivārthe yastyajetprāṇāñchivabhaktārthameva vā  ŚivPab
na tena sadṛśaḥ kaścinmuktimārgasthito naraḥ  ŚivPcd
tasmācchīghratarā muktistasya saṃsāramaṃḍalāt  ŚivPab
eteṣvanyatamopāyaṃ kathamapyavalambya vā  ŚivPcd
ṣaḍadhvaśuddhiṃ vidhivatprāpto vā mriyate yadi  ŚivPab
paśūnāmiva tasyeha na kuryādaurdhvadaihikam  ŚivPcd
naivāśaucaṃ prapadyeta tatputrādiviśeṣataḥ  ŚivPab
śivacārārthamathavā śivavidyārthameva vā  ŚivPcd
khanedvā bhuvi taddehaṃ dahedvā śucināgninā  ŚivPef

athainamapi coddiśya karma cetkartumīpsitam  ŚivPcd
kalyāṇameva kurvīta śaktyā bhaktāṃśca tarpayet  ŚivPab
dhanaṃ tasya bhajecchaivaḥ śaivī cetasya santatiḥ  ŚivPcd
nāsti cettacchive dadyānnadadyātpaśusantatiḥ  ŚivP ef
oṃ iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe śaivayogavarṇanaṃ nāmaikonacatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
Chapter 
śrīsūta uvāca
iti sa vijitamanyoryādavenopamanyoradhigatamabhidhāya jñānayogaṃ munibhyaḥ  ŚivPab
praṇatimupagatebhyastebhya udbhāvitātmā sapadi viyati vāyuḥ sāyamantarhito 'bhūt  ŚivPcd
tataḥ prabhātasamaye naimiṣīyāstapodhanāḥ  ŚivPab
satrānte 'vabhṛthaṃ kartuṃ sarva eva samudyayuḥ  ŚivPcd
tadā brahmasamādeśāddevī sākṣātsarasvatī  ŚivPab
prasannā svādusalilā prāvartata nadīśubhā  ŚivPcd
sarasvatīṃ nadīṃ dṛṣṭvā munayo hṛṣṭamānasāḥ  ŚivPab
samāpya satraṃ prārabdhaṃ cakrustatrāvagāhanam  ŚivPcd
atha saṃtarpya devādīṃstadīyaiḥ salilaiḥ śivaiḥ  ŚivPab
smarantaḥ pūrvavṛttāntaṃ yayurvārāṇasīṃ prati  ŚivPcd
tadā te himavatpādātpaṃtatīṃ dakṣiṇāmukhīm  ŚivPab
dṛṣṭvā bhāgīrathī tatra snātvā tattīrato yayuḥ  ŚivPcd
tato vārāṇasīṃ prāpya muditāssarva eva te  ŚivPab
tadottarapravāhāyāṃ gaṃgāyāmavagāhya ca  ŚivPcd
avimukteśvaraṃ liṃgaṃ dṛṣṭvābhyarcya vidhānataḥ  ŚivPab
prayātumudyatāstatra dadṛśurdivi bhāsvaram  ŚivPcd
sūryakoṭipratīkāśaṃ tejodivyaṃ mahādbhutam  ŚivPab
ātmaprabhāvitānena vyāptasarvadigantaram  ŚivPcd
atha pāśupatāḥ siddhāḥ bhasmasañchannavigrahāḥ  ŚivPab
munayo 'bhyetya śataśo līnāḥ syustatra tejasi  ŚivPcd a
tathā vilīyamāneṣu tapasviṣu mahātmasu  ŚivPab
sadyastirodadhe tejastadadbhutamivābhavat  ŚivPcd
taddṛṣṭvā mahadāścaryaṃ naimiṣīyā maharṣayaḥ  ŚivPab
kimetadityajānanto yayurbrahmavanaṃ prati  ŚivPcd
prāgevaiṣāṃ tu gamanātpavano lokapāvanaḥ  ŚivPab
darśanaṃ naimiṣīyāṇāṃ saṃvādastairmahātmanaḥ  ŚivPcd
śaddhāṃ buddhiṃ tatasteṣāṃ sāṃbe sānucare śive  ŚivPab
samāptiṃ cāpi satrasya dīrghapūrvasya satriṇām  ŚivPcd
vijñāpya jagatāṃ dhātre brahmaṇe brahmayonaye  ŚivPab
svakārye tadanujñāto jagāma svapuraṃ prati  ŚivPcd
atha sthānagato brahmā tumburornāradasya ca  ŚivPab
paraspara spardhitayorgāne vivadamānayoḥ  ŚivPcd
tadudbhāvitagānottharasairmādhyasthamācaran  ŚivPab
gandharvairapsarobhiśca sukhamāste niṣevitaḥ  ŚivPcd
tadānavasarādeva dvāḥsthairdvāri nivāritāḥ  ŚivPab
munayo brahmabhavanādbahiḥ pārśvamupāviśan  ŚivPcd
atha tumburuṇā gāne samatāṃ prāpya nāradaḥ  ŚivPab
sāhacaryeṣvanujñāto brahmaṇā parameṣṭhinā  ŚivPcd
tyaktvā parasparaspardhāṃ maitrīṃ ca paramāṃ gataḥ  ŚivPab
saha tenāpsarobhiśca gandharvaiśca samāvṛtaḥ  ŚivPcd
upavīṇayituṃ devaṃ nakulīśvaramīśvaram  ŚivPab
bhavanānniryayau dhāturjaladādaṃśumāniva  ŚivPcd
taṃ dṛṣṭvā ṣaṭkulīyāste nāradaṃ munigovṛṣam  ŚivPab
praṇamyāvasaraṃ śaṃbhoḥ papracchuḥ paramādarāt  ŚivPcd
sa cāvasara evāyamitoṃtargamyatāmiti  ŚivPab
vadanyayāvanyaparastvarayā parayā yutaḥ  ŚivPcd
tato dvāri sthitā ye vai brahmaṇe tānnyavedayan  ŚivPab
tena te viviśurveśma piṃḍībhūyāṃḍajanmanaḥ  ŚivPcd
praviśya dūrato devaṃ praṇamya bhuvi daṃḍavat  ŚivPab
samīpe tadanujñātāḥ parivṛtyopatasthire  ŚivPcd
tāṃstatrāvasthitān pṛṣṭvā kuśalaṃ kamalāsanaḥ  ŚivPab
vṛttāṃtaṃ vo mayā jñātaṃ vāyurevāha no yataḥ  ŚivPcd
bhavadbhiḥ kiṃ kṛtaṃ paścānmāruteṃtarhite sati  ŚivPab
ityuktavati deveśe munayo 'vabhṛthātparam  ŚivPcd
gaṃgātīrthesya gamanaṃ yātrāṃ vārāṇasīṃ prati  ŚivPab
darśanaṃ tatra liṃgānāṃ sthāpitānāṃ sureśvaraiḥ  ŚivPcd
avimukteśvarasyāpi liṃgasyābhyarcanaṃ sakṛt  ŚivPab
ākāśe mahatastasya tejorāśeśca darśanam  ŚivPcd
munīnāṃ vilayaṃ tatra nirodhaṃ tejasastataḥ  ŚivPab
yāthātmyavedanaṃ tasya ciṃtitasyāpi cātmabhiḥ  ŚivPcd
sarvaṃ savistaraṃ tasmai praṇamyāhurmuhurmuhuḥ  ŚivPab
munibhiḥ kathitaṃ śrutvā viśvakarmā caturmukhaḥ  ŚivPcd
kaṃpayitvā śiraḥ kiṃcitprāha gaṃbhīrayā girā  ŚivPab
pratyāsīdati yuṣmākaṃ siddhirāmuṣmikī parā  ŚivPcd b
bhavadbhirdīrghasatreṇa ciramārādhitaḥ prabhuḥ  ŚivPab
prasādābhimukho bhūta iti bhutārthasūcitam  ŚivPcd
vārāṇasyāṃ tu yuṣmābhiryaddṛṣṭaṃ divi dīptimat  ŚivPab
talliṃgasaṃjñitaṃ sākṣāttejo māheśvaraṃ param  ŚivPcd
tatra līnāśca munayaḥ śrautapāśupatavratāḥ  ŚivPab
muktā babhūvuḥ svasthāśca naiṣṭhikā dagdhakilbiṣāḥ  ŚivPcd
prāpyānena yathā muktiracirādbhavatāmapi  ŚivPab
sa cāyamarthaḥ sūcyeta yuṣmaddṛṣṭena tejasā  ŚivPcd
tatra vaḥ kāla evaiṣa daivādupanataḥ svayam  ŚivPab
prayāta dakṣiṇaṃ meroḥ śikharaṃ devasevitam  ŚivPcd
sanatkumāro yatrāste mama putraḥ paro muniḥ  ŚivPab
pratīkṣyāgamanaṃ sākṣādbhūtanāthasya naṃdinaḥ  ŚivPcd
purā sanatkumāropi dṛṣṭvāpi parameśvaram  ŚivPab
ajñānātsarvayogīndramānī vinayadūṣitaḥ  ŚivPcd
abhyutthānādikaṃ yuktamakurvannatinirbhayaḥ  ŚivPab
tato 'parādhātkruddhena mahoṣṭro naṃdinā kṛtaḥ  ŚivPcd
atha kālena mahatā tadarthe śocatā mayā  ŚivPab
upāsya devaṃ devīñca naṃdinaṃ cānunīya vai  ŚivPcd
kathaṃciduṣṭratā tasya prayatnena nivāritā  ŚivPab
prāpito hi yathāpūrvaṃ sanatpūrvāṃ kumāratām  ŚivPcd
tadāha ca mahādevaḥ smayanniva gaṇādhipam  ŚivPab
avajñāya hi māmeva tathāhaṃkṛtavānmuniḥ  ŚivPcd
atastvameva yāthātmyaṃ mamāsmai kathayānagha  ŚivPab
brahmaṇaḥ pūrvajaḥ putro māṃ mūḍha iva saṃsmaran  ŚivPcd
mayaiva śiṣyate datto mama jñānapravartakaḥ  ŚivPab
dharmādhyakṣābhiṣekaṃ ca tava nirvartayiṣyati  ŚivPcd
sa evaṃ vyāhṛto bhūyassarvabhūtagaṇāgraṇīḥ  ŚivPab
yatparājñāpanaṃ mūrdhnā prātaḥ pratigṛhītavān  ŚivPcd
tathā sanatkumāro 'pi merau madanuśāsanāt  ŚivPab
prasādārthaṃ gaṇasyāsya tapaścarati duścaram  ŚivPcd
draṣṭavyaśceti yuṣmābhiḥ prāggaṇeśasamāgamāt  ŚivPab
tatprasādārthamacirānnaṃdī tatrāgamiṣyati  ŚivPcd
iti satvaramādiśya preṣitā viśvayoginā  ŚivPab
kumāraśikharaṃ merordakṣiṇaṃ munayo yayuḥ  ŚivPcd
oṃ iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe naimiṣarṣiyātrāvarṇanaṃ nāma catvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
Chapter 
sūta uvāca
tatra skaṃdasaro nāma sarassāgarasannibham  ŚivPab
amṛtasvāduśiśirasvacchā gādhalaghūdakam  ŚivPcd
samaṃtataḥ saṃghaṭitaṃ sphaṭiko palasaṃcayaiḥ  ŚivPab
sarvartukusumaiḥ phullaiśchāditākhiladiṅmukham  ŚivPcd
śaivalairutpalaiḥ padmaiḥ kumudaistārakopamaiḥ  ŚivPab
taraṃgairabhrasaṃkāśairākāśamiva bhūmigam  ŚivPcd
sukhāvataraṇārohaiḥ sthalairnīlaśilāmayaiḥ  ŚivPab
sopānamārgau ruciraiśśobhamānāṣṭadiṅmukham  ŚivPcd a
tatrāvatīrṇaiśca yathā tatrottīrṇaśca bhūyasā  ŚivPab
snātaiḥ sitopavītaiśca śuklākaupīnavalkalaiḥ  ŚivPcd
jaṭāśikhāyanairmuṃḍaistripuṃḍrakṛtamaṃḍanaiḥ  ŚivPab
virāgavivaśasmeramukhairmunikumārakaiḥ  ŚivPcd
ghaṭaiḥ kamalinīpatrapuṭaiśca kalaśaiḥ śivaiḥ  ŚivPab
kamaṇḍalubhiranyaiśca tādṛśaiḥ karakādibhiḥ  ŚivPcd
ātmārthaṃ ca parārthaṃ ca devatārthaṃ viśeṣataḥ  ŚivPab
ānīyamānasalilamāttapuṣpaṃ ca nityaśaḥ  ŚivPcd
aṃtarjalaśilārūḍhairnīcānāṃ sparśaśaṃkayā  ŚivPab
ācāravadbhirmunibhiḥ kṛtabhasmāṃgadhūsaraiḥ  ŚivPcd
itastato 'psu majjadbhiriṣṭaśiṣṭaiḥ śilāgataiḥ  ŚivPab
tilaiśca sākṣataiḥ puṣpaistyaktadarbhapavitrakaiḥ  ŚivPcd
devādyamṛṣimadhyaṃ ca nirvartya pitṛtarpaṇam  ŚivPab
nivedayedabhijñebhyo nityasnānagatān dvijān  ŚivPcd
sthānesthāne kṛtānekabalipuṣpasamīraṇaiḥ  ŚivPab
saurārghyapūrvaṃ kurvadbhiḥsthaṃḍalebhyarcanādikam  ŚivPcd
kvacinnimajjadunmajjatprasrastagajayūthapam  ŚivPab
kvacicca tṛṣayāyātamṛgīmṛgaturaṃgamam  ŚivPcd
kvacitpītajanottīrṇamayūravaravāraṇam  ŚivPab
kvacitkṛtataṭāghātavṛṣaprativṛṣojjvalam  ŚivPcd
kvacitkāraṃḍavaravaiḥ kvacitsārasakūjitaiḥ  ŚivPab
kvacicca kokaninadaiḥ kvacidbhramaragītibhiḥ  ŚivPcd
snānapānādikaraṇaiḥ svasaṃpaddrumajīvibhiḥ  ŚivPab
praṇayātprāṇibhistaistairbhāṣamāṇamivāsakṛt  ŚivPcd
kūlaśākhiśikhālīnakokilākulakūjitaiḥ  ŚivPab
ātapopahatānsarvānnāmaṃtrayadivāniśam  ŚivPcd
uttare tasya sarasastīre kalpataroradhaḥ  ŚivPab
vedyāṃ vajraśilāmayyāṃ mṛdule mṛgacarmaṇi  ŚivPcd
sanatkumāramāsīnaṃ śaśvadbālavapurdharam  ŚivPab
tatkālamātroparataṃ samādheracalātmanaḥ  ŚivPcd
upāsyamānaṃ munibhiryogīṃdrairapi pūjitam  ŚivPab
dadṛśurnaimiṣeyāste praṇatāścopatasthire  ŚivPcd
yāvatpṛṣṭavate tasmai procuḥ svāgatakāraṇam  ŚivPab
tumulaḥ śuśruve tāvaddivi duṃdubhinisvanaḥ  ŚivPcd
dadṛśe tatkṣaṇe tasminvimānaṃ bhānusannibham  ŚivPab
gaṇeśvarairasaṃkhyeyaiḥ saṃvṛtaṃ ca samaṃtataḥ  ŚivPcd
apsarogaṇasaṃkīrṇaṃ rudrakanyābhirāvṛtam  ŚivPab
mṛdaṃgamurajodghuṣṭaṃ veṇuvīṇāravānvitam  ŚivPcd
citraratnavitānāḍhyaṃ muktādāmavirājitam  ŚivPab
munibhissiddhagaṃdharvairyakṣacāraṇakinnaraiḥ  ŚivPcd
nṛtyadbhiścaiva gāyadbhirvādayadbhiśca saṃvṛtam  ŚivPab
vīragovṛṣacihnena vidramadrumayaṣṭinā  ŚivPcd
kṛtagopurasatkāraṃ ketunā mānyahetunā  ŚivPab
tasya madhye vimānasya cāmaradvitayāṃtare  ŚivPcd
chattrasya maṇidaṃḍasya caṃdrasyeva śuceradhaḥ  ŚivPab
divyasiṃhāsanārūḍhaṃ devyā suyaśayā saha  ŚivPcd b
śriyā ca vapuṣā caiva tribhiścāpi vilocanaiḥ  ŚivPab
prākārairabhikṛtyānāṃ pratyabhijñāpakaṃ prabhoḥ  ŚivPcd
avilaṃghya jagatkarturājñāpanamivāgatam  ŚivPab
sarvānugrahaṇaṃ śaṃbhoḥ sākṣādiva puraḥsthitam  ŚivPcd
śilādatanayaṃ sākṣācchrīmacchūlavarāyudham  ŚivPab
viśveśvaragaṇādhyakṣaṃ viśveśvaramivāparam  ŚivPcd
viśvasyāpi vidhātḥṇāṃ nigrahānugrahakṣamam  ŚivPab
caturbāhumudārāṃgaṃ candrarekhāvibhūṣitam  ŚivPcd
kaṃṭhe nāgena maulau ca śaśāṃkenāpyalaṃkṛtam  ŚivPab
savigrahamivaiśvaryaṃ sāmarthyamiva sakriyam  ŚivPcd
samāptamiva nirvāṇaṃ sarvajñamiva saṃgatam  ŚivPab
dṛṣṭvā prahṛṣṭavadano brahmaputraḥ saharṣibhiḥ  ŚivPcd
tasthau prāñjalirutthāya tasyātmānamivārpayan  ŚivPab
atha tatrāṃtare tasminvimāne cāvaniṃ gate  ŚivPcd
praṇamya daṇḍavaddevaṃ stutvā vyajñāpayanmunīm  ŚivPab
ṣaṭkulīyā ime dīrghaṃ naimiṣe satramāsthitāḥ  ŚivPcd
āgatā brahmaṇādiṣṭāḥ pūrvamevābhikāṃkṣayā  ŚivPef
śrutvā vākyaṃ brahmaputrasya naṃdīchittvā pāśāndṛṣṭipātena sadyaḥ  ŚivPab
śaivaṃ dharmaṃ caiśvaraṃ jñānayogaṃ dattvā bhūyo devapārśvaṃ jagāma  ŚivPcd
sanatkumāreṇa ca tatsamastaṃ vyāsāya sākṣādgurave mamoktam  ŚivPab
vyāsena coktaṃ mahitena mahyaṃ mayā ca tadvaḥ kathitaṃ samāsāt  ŚivPcd
nāvedavidbhyaḥ kathanīyametatpurāṇaratnaṃ puraśāsanasya  ŚivPab
nābhaktaśiṣyāya ca nāstikebhyo dattaṃ hi mohānnirayaṃ dadāti  ŚivPcd
mārgeṇa sevānugatena yaistaddattaṃ gṛhītaṃ paṭhitaṃ śrutaṃ vā  ŚivPab
tebhyaḥ sukhaṃ dharmamukhaṃ trivargaṃ nirvāṇamaṃte niyataṃ dadāti  ŚivPcd
parasparasyopakṛtaṃ bhavadbhirmayā ca paurāṇikamārgayogāt  ŚivPab
ato gamiṣye 'hamavāptakāmaḥ samastamevāstu śivaṃ sadā naḥ  ŚivPcd
sūte kṛtāśiṣi gate munayaḥ suvṛttā yāge ca paryavasite mahati prayoge  ŚivPab
kāle kalau ca viṣayaiḥ kaluṣāyamāṇe vārāṇasīparisare vasatiṃ vinetuḥ  ŚivPcd
atha ca te paśupāśamumukṣayākhilatayā kṛtapāśupatavratāḥ  ŚivPab
adhikṛtākhilabodhasamādhayaḥ paramanirvṛtimāpuraniṃditāḥ  ŚivPcd
vyāsa uvāca
etacchivapurāṇaṃ hi samāptaṃ hitamādarāt  ŚivPab
paṭhitavyaṃ prayatnena śrotavyaṃ ca tathaiva hi  ŚivPcd
nāstikāya na vaktavyamaśraddhāya śaṭhāya ca  ŚivPab
abhaktāya maheśasya tathā dharmadhvajāya ca  ŚivPcd
etacchrutyā hyekavāraṃ bhavetpāpaṃ hi bhasmasāt  ŚivPab
abhakto bhaktimāpnoti bhakto bhaktisamṛddhibhāk  ŚivPcd
punaḥ śrute ca sadbhaktirmuktissyācca śruteḥ punaḥ  ŚivPab
tasmātpunaḥpunaścaiva śrotavyaṃ hi mumukṣubhiḥ  ŚivPcd a
pañcāvṛttiḥ prakartavyā purāṇasyāsya saddhiyā  ŚivPab
paraṃ phalaṃ samuddiśya tatprāpnoti na saṃśayaḥ  ŚivPcd
purātanāśca rājāno viprā vaiśyāśca sattamāḥ  ŚivPab
saptakṛtvastadāvṛttyālabhanta śivadarśanam  ŚivPcd
śroṣyatyathāpi yaścedaṃ mānavo bhaktitatparaḥ  ŚivPab
iha bhuktvākhilānbhogānaṃte muktiṃ labhecca saḥ  ŚivPcd
etacchivapurāṇaṃ hi śivasyātipriyaṃ param  ŚivPab
bhuktimuktipradaṃ brahmasaṃmitaṃ bhaktivardhanam  ŚivPcd
etacchivapurāṇasya vaktuḥ śrotuśca sarvadā  ŚivPab
sagaṇassasutassāṃbaśśaṃ karotu sa śaṃkaraḥ  ŚivPcd
oṃ iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe vyāsopadeśaśrīśivamahāpurāṇamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāmaikacatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
samāpto 'yaṃ granthaḥ
